--- Commit Message ---
LU-13064 sec: check permissions for changelogs access

root permissions should be checked when reading or clearing changelogs
from clients. In particular, if root is squashed via a nodemap entry,
it should not be allowed to access changelogs.
To achieve this send mdt body along with RQF_LLOG_ORIGIN_HANDLE_CREATE
and RQF_MDT_SET_INFO requests. And on server side, retrieve user
credentials and make sure they have root permission.

Test-Parameters: clientversion=2.12 envdefinitions=SANITY_EXCEPT="27M 56ra 151 156 802"
Test-Parameters: serverversion=2.12
Signed-off-by: Sebastien Buisson <sbuisson@ddn.com>

 > land.
 > The problem in lustre-initialization is due to newly introduced

You could rebase your patches to be on top of 38107, so long as you do not cause it to be updated (otherwise it would restart testing, which may further delay landing).

You can do that directly in Gerrit by selecting "Rebase" for the *bottom* patch in your series, and checking "Change parent version" and putting 38107 in there and then "Rebase" for each patch above it. Alternately, using "Download->checkout" on the 38107 patch and then rebasing your patch series onto that patch and pushing it to Gerrit again (after verifying the Git hash of the 38107 patch is still the same as Gerrit).
